%d-%d-%d-%d-%d-%d-%d-%d-%d-%d
	Set fixed RateInfo string as %s
Parameter Usage:
	iwpriv ra0 set assoc=[mac:hh:hh:hh:hh:hh:hh]-[wtbl:dd]-[ownmac:dd]-[type:xx]-[mode:mmm]-[bw:dd]-[nss:ss]-[maxrate:kkk_dd]
		mac: peer's mac address in hex format
			Example=> mac:00:0c:43:12:34:56
		wtbl: the WTBL entry index peer will occupied, in range 1~127
			Example=> wtbl:1
		ownmac: the OwnMAC index we'll used to send frame to this peer, in range 0~4 or 16~31
			Example=> ownmac:0
		type: peer's operation type, is a ap or sta, allow input: "ap" or "sta"
			Example=> type:ap
		mode: peer's phy operation mode, allow input: a/b/g/gn/an/ac
			Example=> mode:aanac	to indicate peer can support A/AN/AC mode
		bw: Peer's bandwidth capability, in range to 20/40/80/160
			Example=> bw:40	indicate peer can support BW_40
		nss: Peer's capability for Spatial stream which can tx/rx, in range of 1~4 with restriction of Software/Hardware cap.
			Example=> nss:2	indicate peer can support 2ss for both tx/rx
		maxrate: Peer's data rate capability for tx/rx, separate as two parts and separate by '_' character
				 kkk: phy modulation mode, allow input:'cck', 'ofdm', 'htmix', 'htgf', 'vht'
				 dd:phy mcs rate, for CCK:0~3, OFDM:0~7, HT:0~32, VHT:0~9
			Example=> maxrate:cck_1	indicate we only can transmit CCK and MCS 1(2Mbps) or lower MCS to peer
			Example=> maxrate:ofdm_3	indicate we only can transmit OFDM and MCS 3(24Mbps) to peer
			Example=> maxrate:htmix_3	indicate we only can transmit OFDM and MCS 3(24Mbps) to peer

=============================================================================================
                            ATE ETxBF Certification Procedure Guide
For HT20 mode
 1)  iwpriv ra0 set ATEEBFCE=1
 2)  iwpriv ra0 set ATEConTxETxBfGdProc=02:00:00:036:112:1 (Use in Golden Device)
 3)  iwpriv ra0 set ATEConTxETxBfInitProc=02:00:00:01:04:18:036:112:1:04000
 4)  iwpriv ra0 set ATETXEBF=1 (Tx packet apply BF On)
 5)  iwpriv ra0 set ATE=TXFRAME
 6)  iwpriv ra0 mac 820fa09c (check [15:0] eBF counter, if apply then nonzero)
 7)  check IQxel waveform
 8)  iwpriv ra0 set ATETXEBF=0 (Tx packet apply BF Off)
 9)  iwpriv ra0 mac 820fa09c (check [15:0] eBF counter, if not apply then zero)
10)  check Iqxel waveformn
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
For HT40 mode
 2)  iwpriv ra0 set ATEConTxETxBfGdProc=02:00:01:036:112:1 (Use in Golden Device)
 3)  iwpriv ra0 set ATEConTxETxBfInitProc=02:00:01:01:04:18:036:112:1:04000
 5)  iwpriv ra0 set ATE=TXFRAMESKB
10)  check Iqxel waveform
For VHT80 mode
 2)  iwpriv ra0 set ATEConTxETxBfGdProc=04:00:02:036:112:1 (Use in Golden Device)
 3)  iwpriv ra0 set ATEConTxETxBfInitProc=04:00:02:01:04:18:036:112:1:16000
For VHT160C mode
 2)  iwpriv ra0 set ATEConTxETxBfGdProc=04:00:03:036:112:1 (Use in Golden Device)
 3)  iwpriv ra0 set ATEConTxETxBfInitProc=04:00:03:01:04:18:036:112:1:16000
For VHT160NC mode
 2)  iwpriv ra0 set ATEConTxETxBfGdProc=04:00:06:036:112:1 (Use in Golden Device)
 3)  iwpriv ra0 set ATEConTxETxBfInitProc=04:00:06:01:04:18:036:112:1:16000
For DBDC Band1 HT20 mode
 1)  configure DBDC mode and Reboot system
 2)  iwpriv ra1 set ATEEBFCE=1
 3)  iwpriv ra1 set ATEConTxETxBfGdProc=02:00:00:36:112:1 (Use in Golden Device)
 4)  iwpriv ra1 set ATEConTxETxBfInitProc=02:00:00:01:02:18:36:112:1:04000
 5)  iwpriv ra1 set ATETXEBF=1 (Tx packet apply BF On)
 6)  iwpriv ra1 set ATE=TXFRAMESKB
 7)  iwpriv ra1 mac 820fa09c (check [15:0] eBF counter, if apply then nonzero)
 8)  check IQxel waveform
 9)  iwpriv ra1 set ATETXEBF=0 (Tx packet apply BF Off)
10)  iwpriv ra1 mac 820fa09c (check [15:0] eBF counter, if not apply then zero)
11)  check Iqxel waveform
                           Method for Dynamical Control Tx Power
 1)  Follow ETxBF Certification Procedure to enable TxBf packet at first
 2)  Use command "iwpriv ra0 set ATE=TXSTOP" to stop Tx
 3)  Use command "iwpriv ra0 set ATETXPOW0=XX" to configure Tx Power DAC value for OFDM 54M
 4)  USe command "ra0 set ATE=TXFRAMESKB" to start continuous packet Tx
ATE=ATESTART, ATESTOP, TXCONT, TXCARR, TXCARS, TXFRAME, RXFRAME
ATEDA
ATESA
ATEBSSID
ATECHANNEL, range:0~14
ATETXPOW0, set power level of antenna 1.
ATETXPOW1, set power level of antenna 2.
ATETXANT, set TX antenna. 0:all, 1:antenna one, 2:antenna two.
ATERXANT, set RX antenna.0:all, 1:antenna one, 2:antenna two, 3:antenna three.
ATETXBW, set BandWidth, 0:20MHz, 1:40MHz
ATETXLEN, set Frame length, range 24~%d
ATETXCNT, set how many frame going to transmit.
ATETXMCS, set MCS, reference to rate table.
ATETXMODE, set Mode 0:CCK, 1:OFDM, 2:HT-Mix, 3:GreenField, 4:VHT, reference to rate table.
ATETXGI, set GI interval, 0:Long, 1:Short
ATERXFER, 0:disable Rx Frame error rate. 1:enable Rx Frame error rate.
ATERRF, show all RF registers.
ATELDE2P, load EEPROM from .bin file.
ATERE2P, display all EEPROM content.
ATEAUTOALC, enable ATE auto Tx alc (Tx auto level control).
ATEIPG, set ATE Tx frame IPG.
ATEPAYLOAD, set ATE payload pattern for TxFrame.
ATESHOW, display all parameters of ATE.
ATEHELP, online help.
